### Development Step 7: Access 2020 Nature.com Chinstrap Penguin Global Population Study; Extract Figures and Methodology

**Description**: Search for and access the Nature.com article titled 'global population assessment of the Chinstrap penguin' from 2020. Extract the specific population figure from this study, noting whether it's provided as breeding pairs or individual penguins. Document the exact methodology and population count to enable accurate comparison with the Wikipedia 2018 data.

**Use Cases**:
- Wildlife conservation policy development and regulatory compliance tracking for environmental agencies extracting Chinstrap penguin counts and survey methods to inform protected area management
- Automated meta-analysis pipeline for ecological research labs harvesting 2020 population figures and methodologies for comparative species trend studies
- Environmental NGO report generation and stakeholder presentations incorporating precise breeding-pair data from Nature studies into annual conservation impact reports
- Marine biology curriculum content creation using extracted global population figures and field census techniques as real-world case studies for university courses
- Integration of structured penguin population data into open biodiversity platforms and JSON databases to support public research and citizen science initiatives
- Climate change impact modeling workflow for research institutes feeding standardized population metrics into ecosystem simulation models to forecast Antarctic biodiversity shifts
- Journalistic fact-checking and science news enrichment verifying reported Chinstrap penguin numbers and methodology details when covering Nature.com publications
- Automated updates to Wikipedia species entries comparing 2020 Nature study data with 2018 figures and generating structured update recommendations for editors

```
import os
import re
import json

print("=== PARSING 2020 NATURE STUDY FOR POPULATION FIGURES ===\n")

# Locate workspace directory
workspace_dirs = [d for d in os.listdir('.') if d.startswith('workspace')]
if not workspace_dirs:
print("No workspace directory found.")
exit()

workspace_dir = workspace_dirs[0]
print(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\n")

# Load the correct 2020 study text file
study_text_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'nature_chinstrap_2020_study_text.txt')
if not os.path.exists(study_text_file):
print(f"Study text file not found: {study_text_file}")
exit()

print(f"Reading study text file: {os.path.basename(study_text_file)}")
with open(study_text_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
study_text = f.read()

print(f"Study text length: {len(study_text):,} characters\n")

# First, let's examine the overall structure and find key sections
print("=== IDENTIFYING KEY SECTIONS IN THE STUDY ===\n")

# Look for major section headings
section_patterns = [
r'Abstract',
r'Introduction',
r'Results',
r'Discussion',
r'Methods',
r'Conclusion'
]

found_sections = []
for pattern in section_patterns:
matches = list(re.finditer(pattern, study_text, re.IGNORECASE))
if matches:
for match in matches:
found_sections.append({
'section': pattern,
'position': match.start(),
'text': match.group()
})

# Sort sections by position
found_sections.sort(key=lambda x: x['position'])

print("Major sections found:")
for section in found_sections:
print(f" - {section['section']} at position {section['position']:,}")

# Extract key population-related numbers and methodology
print("\n=== SEARCHING FOR POPULATION FIGURES ===\n")

# Patterns to look for population numbers
population_patterns = [
r'(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(?:breeding\s*pairs?|pairs?)',
r'(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(?:individuals?|penguins?)',
r'population\s+of\s+(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)',
r'total\s+(?:of\s+)?(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(?:breeding\s*pairs?|pairs?|individuals?)',
r'estimated\s+(?:at\s+)?(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(?:breeding\s*pairs?|pairs?|individuals?)',
r'global\s+population\s+(?:of\s+)?(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)',
r'approximately\s+(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(?:breeding\s*pairs?|pairs?|individuals?)'
]

population_findings = []

for pattern in population_patterns:
matches = list(re.finditer(pattern, study_text, re.IGNORECASE))
for match in matches:
# Get context around the match (200 characters before and after)
start = max(0, match.start() - 200)
end = min(len(study_text), match.end() + 200)
context = study_text[start:end]

population_findings.append({
'pattern': pattern,
'match': match.group(),
'number': match.group(1) if match.groups() else 'N/A',
'position': match.start(),
'context': context.replace('\n', ' ').strip()
})

print(f"Found {len(population_findings)} potential population references:")
for i, finding in enumerate(population_findings, 1):
print(f"\nFinding {i}:")
print(f" Match: {finding['match']}")
print(f" Number: {finding['number']}")
print(f" Position: {finding['position']:,}")
print(f" Context: ...{finding['context'][:300]}...")

# Look specifically for key result statements
print("\n=== SEARCHING FOR KEY RESULT STATEMENTS ===\n")

# Look for sentences containing key result phrases
result_patterns = [
r'[^.]*global\s+population[^.]*\.',
r'[^.]*breeding\s+pairs?[^.]*\d[^.]*\.',
r'[^.]*total[^.]*population[^.]*\d[^.]*\.',
r'[^.]*census[^.]*\d[^.]*\.',
r'[^.]*estimate[^.]*\d[^.]*breeding[^.]*\.',
r'[^.]*\d[^.]*million[^.]*pairs?[^.]*\.'
]

key_statements = []
for pattern in result_patterns:
matches = list(re.finditer(pattern, study_text, re.IGNORECASE | re.DOTALL))
for match in matches:
statement = match.group().strip()
# Clean up the statement
statement = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', statement)

key_statements.append({
'pattern': pattern,
'statement': statement,
'position': match.start()
})

print(f"Found {len(key_statements)} key result statements:")
for i, stmt in enumerate(key_statements, 1):
print(f"\nStatement {i}:")
print(f" Position: {stmt['position']:,}")
print(f" Text: {stmt['statement']}")

# Look for methodology section
print("\n=== EXTRACTING METHODOLOGY INFORMATION ===\n")

# Find methods section
methods_match = re.search(r'Methods?\s*\n?([\s\S]*?)(?=\n\s*(?:Results?|Discussion|Conclusion|References?|Acknowledgments?)\s*\n|$)', study_text, re.IGNORECASE)

if methods_match:
methods_text = methods_match.group(1)[:2000] # First 2000 characters
print("Methods section found (first 2000 characters):")
print(methods_text)

# Look for specific methodology terms
method_terms = ['survey', 'census', 'count', 'observation', 'field', 'colony', 'site']
found_method_terms = [term for term in method_terms if term.lower() in methods_text.lower()]
print(f"\nMethodology terms found: {found_method_terms}")
else:
print("Methods section not clearly identified")

# Look for abstract for concise population summary
print("\n=== EXTRACTING ABSTRACT FOR POPULATION SUMMARY ===\n")

abstract_match = re.search(r'Abstract\s*\n?([\s\S]*?)(?=\n\s*(?:Introduction|Keywords?)\s*\n|$)', study_text, re.IGNORECASE)

if abstract_match:
abstract_text = abstract_match.group(1)[:1500] # First 1500 characters
print("Abstract found (first 1500 characters):")
print(abstract_text)

# Extract numbers from abstract
abstract_numbers = re.findall(r'\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*(?:\.\d+)?', abstract_text)
print(f"\nNumbers found in abstract: {abstract_numbers}")
else:
print("Abstract section not clearly identified")

# Save comprehensive analysis
analysis_results = {
'study_info': {
'title': 'A global population assessment of the Chinstrap penguin (Pygoscelis antarctica)',
'year': 2020,
'source': 'Nature.com Scientific Reports',
'text_length': len(study_text)
},
'sections_found': found_sections,
'population_findings': population_findings,
'key_statements': key_statements,
'methods_text': methods_text if 'methods_text' in locals() else 'Not extracted',
'abstract_text': abstract_text if 'abstract_text' in locals() else 'Not extracted',
'abstract_numbers': abstract_numbers if 'abstract_numbers' in locals() else []
}

analysis_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'nature_2020_population_analysis.json')
with open(analysis_file, 'w') as f:
json.dump(analysis_results, f, indent=2, default=str)

print(f"\n=== ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===\n")
print(f"Comprehensive analysis saved to: {analysis_file}")
print(f"Population findings: {len(population_findings)}")
print(f"Key statements: {len(key_statements)}")
print(f"Sections identified: {len(found_sections)}")

print("\nNext step: Review findings to identify the specific global population figure and methodology")
```

### Development Step 5: Access 2020 Nature.com Chinstrap Penguin Population Study: Extract Count & Methodology for 2018 Comparison

**Description**: Search for and access the Nature.com article titled 'global population assessment of the Chinstrap penguin' from 2020. Extract the specific population figure from this study, noting whether it's provided as breeding pairs or individual penguins. Document the exact methodology and population count to enable accurate comparison with the Wikipedia 2018 data.

**Use Cases**:
- Wildlife conservation NGOs sourcing the latest Chinstrap penguin population figures and methodologies to prioritize colony protection efforts in Antarctica
- University ecology researchers comparing 2020 Nature.com breeding pair estimates with 2018 Wikipedia counts for peer-reviewed longitudinal studies on penguin demographics
- Environmental consultants integrating authoritative Chinstrap penguin numbers into Antarctic tourism impact assessments for compliance with sustainability regulations
- Automated monitoring pipelines extracting updated population data and sampling methods to trigger alerts when Chinstrap penguin counts deviate beyond threshold in ecological dashboards
- Data journalism teams retrieving precise penguin population metrics and survey techniques to create interactive articles on wildlife conservation trends
- Government wildlife agencies extracting standardized population figures from peer-reviewed studies to inform national biodiversity action plans and policy decisions
- E-learning content developers incorporating verified Chinstrap penguin population data and research methods into interactive modules on polar ecosystems
- Citizen science platforms validating volunteer-submitted colony count data against professional population assessments for accuracy and training feedback

```
import os
import re
import requests
import json
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

print("=== SEARCHING FOR NATURE.COM CHINSTRAP PENGUIN POPULATION STUDY (2020) ===\n")

# Search for the specific Nature.com article about Chinstrap penguin global population assessment from 2020
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
print("API key found. Proceeding with search...\n")

# Construct specific search query for Nature.com Chinstrap penguin study
query = 'site:nature.com "global population assessment" "Chinstrap penguin" 2020'

print(f"Search query: {query}")

# Prepare API request parameters
params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": 10,
"type": "search"
}

# Make API request to SerpAPI
print("\nMaking search request...")
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()
print(f"Search completed successfully. Status code: {response.status_code}")

# Check if we have organic results
if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"\nFound {len(results['organic_results'])} search results:\n")

nature_articles = []

for i, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'], 1):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f"Result {i}:")
print(f" Title: {title}")
print(f" URL: {link}")
print(f" Snippet: {snippet}")
print()

# Check if this is a Nature.com article about Chinstrap penguins
if ('nature.com' in link.lower() and
('chinstrap' in title.lower() or 'chinstrap' in snippet.lower()) and
('population' in title.lower() or 'population' in snippet.lower()) and
'2020' in (title + snippet)):

nature_articles.append({
'title': title,
'url': link,
'snippet': snippet,
'result_number': i
})
print(f" *** IDENTIFIED AS TARGET NATURE ARTICLE ***")

# Save search results for reference
search_results_data = {
'search_query': query,
'total_results': len(results['organic_results']),
'nature_articles_found': len(nature_articles),
'all_results': results['organic_results'],
'identified_nature_articles': nature_articles
}

with open('workspace/nature_chinstrap_search_results.json', 'w') as f:
json.dump(search_results_data, f, indent=2)

print(f"\n=== SEARCH RESULTS SUMMARY ===")
print(f"Total search results: {len(results['organic_results'])}")
print(f"Nature.com articles identified: {len(nature_articles)}")

if nature_articles:
print("\n=== IDENTIFIED NATURE.COM ARTICLES ===")
for article in nature_articles:
print(f"\nArticle {article['result_number']}:")
print(f"Title: {article['title']}")
print(f"URL: {article['url']}")
print(f"Snippet: {article['snippet']}")

# Try to access the first Nature article found
target_article = nature_articles[0]
print(f"\n=== ATTEMPTING TO ACCESS TARGET ARTICLE ===")
print(f"Target URL: {target_article['url']}")

# Set up headers to mimic browser request
headers = {
'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36',

]

break

if article_content:

print(f"\nExtracted content length: {len(content_text):,} characters")

else:

import os import requests import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import time print("=== SEARCHING FOR NATURE JOURNAL 2020 PUBLICATION STATISTICS ===\n") # First, try searching for bibliometric reports and journal statistics api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found. Proceeding with search...\n") # Multiple search strategies to find Nature's 2020 publication count search_queries = [ 'Nature journal "2020" "articles published" "research articles" count statistics', 'Nature publishing "journal impact factor" 2020 "number of articles"', 'bibliometric analysis Nature journal 2020 publication count', 'Web of Science Scopus Nature journal 2020 article statistics', 'Nature journal annual report 2020 publications research articles' ] all_search_results = [] for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"Search {i}/5: {query}") params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 10, "type": "search" } try: response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f" Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results") # Store results with search context search_batch = { 'search_number': i, 'query': query, 'results_count': len(results['organic_results']), 'results': results['organic_results'] } all_search_results.append(search_batch) # Look for promising results in this batch promising_results = [] for result in results['organic_results']: title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() url = result.get('link', '').lower() # Check for bibliometric databases or journal statistics if any(keyword in (title + snippet + url) for keyword in [ 'web of science', 'scopus', 'pubmed', 'bibliometric', 'journal impact', 'citation report', 'clarivate', 'elsevier', 'nature.com/articles', 'annual report' ]): promising_results.append(result) if promising_results: print(f" *** Found {len(promising_results)} promising results in this batch ***") for j, result in enumerate(promising_results[:3], 1): print(f" {j}. {result.get('title')[:80]}...") print(f" URL: {result.get('link')}") else: print(" No results found") else: print(f" Search failed with status {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f" Error in search {i}: {e}") # Small delay between searches time.sleep(1) print() # Save all search results os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) search_results_file = 'workspace/nature_2020_publication_search_results.json' with open(search_results_file, 'w') as f: json.dump({ 'search_timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'total_searches': len(search_queries), 'search_batches': all_search_results }, f, indent=2) print(f"=== SEARCH RESULTS SUMMARY ===\n") print(f"Total searches conducted: {len(all_search_results)}") print(f"Search results saved to: {search_results_file}") # Analyze all results to find the most promising sources all_promising_results = [] for batch in all_search_results: for result in batch['results']: title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() url = result.get('link', '').lower() # Score results based on relevance indicators score = 0 relevance_indicators = { 'web of science': 10, 'scopus': 10, 'clarivate': 8, 'bibliometric': 7, 'journal impact factor': 6, 'nature.com': 5, 'annual report': 5, 'publication statistics': 8, 'research articles': 6, 'article count': 7, '2020': 3 } for indicator, weight in relevance_indicators.items(): if indicator in (title + snippet + url): score += weight if score >= 10: # Threshold for promising results all_promising_results.append({ 'title': result.get('title'), 'url': result.get('link'), 'snippet': result.get('snippet'), 'relevance_score': score, 'search_query': batch['query'] }) # Sort by relevance score all_promising_results.sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) print(f"\n=== TOP PROMISING RESULTS (Score >= 10) ===\n") print(f"Found {len(all_promising_results)} high-relevance results:\n") for i, result in enumerate(all_promising_results[:10], 1): print(f"Result {i} (Score: {result['relevance_score']})") print(f" Title: {result['title']}") print(f" URL: {result['url']}") print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet'][:150]}...") print(f" Found via: {result['search_query'][:50]}...") print() # import os import requests import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import time print("=== SEARCHING FOR NATURE JOURNAL 2020 PUBLICATION STATISTICS ===\n") # First, try searching for bibliometric reports and journal statistics api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found. Proceeding with search...\n") # Multiple search strategies to find Nature's 2020 publication count search_queries = [ 'Nature journal "2020" "articles published" "research articles" count statistics', 'Nature publishing "journal impact factor" 2020 "number of articles"', 'bibliometric analysis Nature journal 2020 publication count', 'Web of Science Scopus Nature journal 2020 article statistics', 'Nature journal annual report 2020 publications research articles' ] all_search_results = [] for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"Search {i}/5: {query}") params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 10, "type": "search" } try: response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f" Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results") # Store results with search context search_batch = { 'search_number': i, 'query': query, 'results_count': len(results['organic_results']), 'results': results['organic_results'] } all_search_results.append(search_batch) # Look for promising results in this batch promising_results = [] for result in results['organic_results']: title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() url = result.get('link', '').lower() # Check for bibliometric databases or journal statistics if any(keyword in (title + snippet + url) for keyword in [ 'web of science', 'scopus', 'pubmed', 'bibliometric', 'journal impact', 'citation report', 'clarivate', 'elsevier', 'nature.com/articles', 'annual report' ]): promising_results.append(result) if promising_results: print(f" *** Found {len(promising_results)} promising results in this batch ***") for j, result in enumerate(promising_results[:3], 1): print(f" {j}. {result.get('title')[:80]}...") print(f" URL: {result.get('link')}") else: print(" No results found") else: print(f" Search failed with status {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f" Error in search {i}: {e}") # Small delay between searches time.sleep(1) print() # Save all search results os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) search_results_file = 'workspace/nature_2020_publication_search_results.json' with open(search_results_file, 'w') as f: json.dump({ 'search_timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'total_searches': len(search_queries), 'search_batches': all_search_results }, f, indent=2) print(f"=== SEARCH RESULTS SUMMARY ===\n") print(f"Total searches conducted: {len(all_search_results)}") print(f"Search results saved to: {search_results_file}") # Analyze all results to find the most promising sources all_promising_results = [] for batch in all_search_results: for result in batch['results']: title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() url = result.get('link', '').lower() # Score results based on relevance indicators score = 0 relevance_indicators = { 'web of science': 10, 'scopus': 10, 'clarivate': 8, 'bibliometric': 7, 'journal impact factor': 6, 'nature.com': 5, 'annual report': 5, 'publication statistics': 8, 'research articles': 6, 'article count': 7, '2020': 3 } for indicator, weight in relevance_indicators.items(): if indicator in (title + snippet + url): score += weight if score >= 10: # Threshold for promising results all_promising_results.append({ 'title': result.get('title'), 'url': result.get('link'), 'snippet': result.get('snippet'), 'relevance_score': score, 'search_query': batch['query'] }) # Sort by relevance score all_promising_results.sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) print(f"\n=== TOP PROMISING RESULTS (Score >= 10) ===\n") print(f"Found {len(all_promising_results)} high-relevance results:\n") for i, result in enumerate(all_promising_results[:10], 1): print(f"Result {i} (Score: {result['relevance_score']})") print(f" Title: {result['title']}") print(f" URL: {result['url']}") print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet'][:150]}...") print(f" Found via: {result['search_query'][:50]}...") print() # Try to access the most promising results if all_promising_results: print(f"=== ATTEMPTING TO ACCESS TOP RESULTS ===\n") headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate', 'Connection': 'keep-alive' } successful_accesses = [] for i, result in enumerate(all_promising_results[:5], 1): print(f"Accessing result {i}: {result['title'][:60]}...") print(f"URL: {result['url']}") try: response = requests.get(result['url'], headers=headers, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: print(f" ‚úì Successfully accessed (Status: {response.status_code})") print(f" Content length: {len(response.content):,} bytes") # Save the content for analysis filename = f"workspace/nature_source_{i}_{result['relevance_score']}.html" with open(filename, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f" Content saved to: {filename}") # Quick analysis for publication count mentions soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') text_content = soup.get_text().lower() # Look for potential publication counts import re # Patterns that might indicate article counts for Nature in 2020 count_patterns = [ r'nature.*2020.*?(\d{1,4}).*?articles?', r'2020.*?nature.*?(\d{1,4}).*?articles?', r'articles?.*?published.*?nature.*?2020.*?(\d{1,4})', r'nature.*?published.*?(\d{1,4}).*?articles?.*?2020', r'research.*?articles?.*?nature.*?2020.*?(\d{1,4})' ] potential_counts = [] for pattern in count_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, text_content) if matches: potential_counts.extend(matches) if potential_counts: print(f" *** Potential article counts found: {set(potential_counts)} ***") successful_accesses.append({ 'result_info': result, 'filename': filename, 'content_length': len(response.content), 'potential_counts': list(set(potential_counts)) }) else: print(f" ‚úó Access failed (Status: {response.status_code})") except Exception as e: print(f" ‚úó Error accessing: {e}") print() time.sleep(2) # Respectful delay # Save successful access summary access_summary = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'successful_accesses': len(successful_accesses), 'accessed_sources': successful_accesses } summary_file = 'workspace/nature_2020_access_summary.json' with open(summary_file, 'w') as f: json.dump(access_summary, f, indent=2) print(f"=== ACCESS SUMMARY ===\n") print(f"Successfully accessed: {len(successful_accesses)} sources") print(f"Access summary saved to: {summary_file}") if successful_accesses: print(f"\nFiles created in workspace/:") for access in successful_accesses: print(f" - {access['filename']} ({access['content_length']:,} bytes)") if access['potential_counts']: print(f" Potential counts found: {access['potential_counts']}") else: print("No highly relevant results found. May need to try alternative search strategies.") print(f"\n=== INITIAL SEARCH PHASE COMPLETE ===\n") print("Next steps:") print("1. Analyze downloaded content for Nature 2020 publication statistics") print("2. Look for bibliometric databases or journal reports") print("3. Search for Web of Science or Scopus data if accessible") print("4. Try direct searches on Nature.com for annual reports or statistics")

Python Code python
import os import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re print("=== ANALYZING DOWNLOADED SOURCES FOR NATURE 2020 PUBLICATION DATA ===\n") # Find workspace directory workspace_dirs = [d for d in os.listdir('.') if d.startswith('workspace')] if not workspace_dirs: print("No workspace directory found.") exit() workspace_dir = workspace_dirs[0] print(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\n") # First, inspect the access summary file structure access_summary_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'nature_2020_access_summary.json') if os.path.exists(access_summary_file): print("=== INSPECTING ACCESS SUMMARY STRUCTURE ===\n") with open(access_summary_file, 'r') as f: access_data = json.load(f) print("Top-level keys in access summary:") for key, value in access_data.items(): if isinstance(value, list): print(f" {key}: List with {len(value)} items") elif isinstance(value, dict): print(f" {key}: Dictionary") else: print(f" {key}: {value}") if 'accessed_sources' in access_data: print(f"\nAccessed sources structure:") for i, source in enumerate(access_data['accessed_sources'], 1): print(f" Source {i}:") for key, value in source.items(): if key == 'result_info': print(f" {key}: {type(value).__name__} with keys: {list(value.keys()) if isinstance(value, dict) else 'N/A'}") else: print(f" {key}: {value}") else: print("Access summary file not found.") print("\n=== ANALYZING DOWNLOADED HTML FILES ===\n") # Get list of downloaded HTML files html_files = [f for f in os.listdir(workspace_dir) if f.endswith('.html') and 'nature_source' in f] print(f"Found {len(html_files)} HTML files to analyze:\n") for filename in html_files: print(f" - {filename}") analysis_results = [] for filename in html_files: print(f"\n=== ANALYZING {filename} ===\n") file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, filename) file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f"File size: {file_size:,} bytes") try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: html_content = f.read() # Parse with BeautifulSoup soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Extract title title_tag = soup.find('title') page_title = title_tag.get_text().strip() if title_tag else 'No title found' print(f"Page title: {page_title}") # Extract main text content text_content = soup.get_text() print(f"Text content length: {len(text_content):,} characters") # Search for Nature journal publication statistics print("\n--- Searching for Nature publication data ---") # Multiple search patterns for Nature 2020 article counts nature_patterns = [ r'nature.*?(?:journal|publishing).*?2020.*?(\d{1,4}).*?(?:articles?|papers?|publications?)', r'2020.*?nature.*?(\d{1,4}).*?(?:articles?|papers?|publications?)', r'(?:articles?|papers?).*?published.*?nature.*?2020.*?(\d{1,4})', r'nature.*?published.*?(\d{1,4}).*?(?:articles?|papers?).*?2020', r'research.*?(?:articles?|papers?).*?nature.*?2020.*?(\d{1,4})', r'nature.*?(?:volume|vol).*?2020.*?(\d{1,4}).*?(?:articles?|issues?)', r'impact.*?factor.*?nature.*?2020.*?(\d{1,4})', r'journal.*?statistics.*?nature.*?2020.*?(\d{1,4})' ] found_numbers = set() pattern_matches = [] text_lower = text_content.lower() for pattern in nature_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, text_lower, re.IGNORECASE | re.DOTALL) if matches: for match in matches: found_numbers.add(match) # Get context around the match match_pos = text_lower.find(match.lower()) if match_pos != -1: start = max(0, match_pos - 100) end = min(len(text_content), match_pos + 100) context = text_content[start:end].replace('\n', ' ').strip() pattern_matches.append({ 'pattern': pattern, 'number': match, 'context': context }) if found_numbers: print(f"*** Found potential Nature article counts: {sorted(found_numbers)} ***") for match in pattern_matches[:5]: # Show first 5 matches print(f" Number: {match['number']}") print(f" Context: ...{match['context'][:200]}...") print() else: print("No specific Nature article counts found") # Look for bibliometric data tables or structured data print("\n--- Searching for bibliometric data ---") # Look for tables that might contain journal statistics tables = soup.find_all('table') print(f"Found {len(tables)} tables in the document") table_data = [] for i, table in enumerate(tables[:3], 1): # Check first 3 tables table_text = table.get_text().lower() if 'nature' in table_text and ('2020' in table_text or 'articles' in table_text): print(f"*** Table {i} contains Nature-related data ***") # Extract table content rows = table.find_all('tr') if rows: table_content = [] for row in rows[:10]: # First 10 rows cells = [cell.get_text().strip() for cell in row.find_all(['td', 'th'])] if cells: table_content.append(cells) table_data.append({ 'table_number': i, 'rows': table_content }) print(f" Sample rows from table {i}:") for j, row in enumerate(table_content[:5], 1): print(f" Row {j}: {row}") # Look for specific keywords that might indicate journal statistics print("\n--- Searching for journal statistics keywords ---") stat_keywords = [ 'journal impact factor', 'articles published', 'publication count', 'research articles', 'annual statistics', 'bibliometric data', 'citation report', 'journal metrics', 'publication statistics' ] found_keywords = [] for keyword in stat_keywords: if keyword in text_lower: found_keywords.append(keyword) # Get context keyword_pos = text_lower.find(keyword) if keyword_pos != -1: start = max(0, keyword_pos - 150) end = min(len(text_content), keyword_pos + 150) context = text_content[start:end].replace('\n', ' ').strip() print(f" Found '{keyword}': ...{context}...") print(f"Keywords found: {found_keywords}") # Store analysis results file_analysis = { 'filename': filename, 'file_size': file_size, 'page_title': page_title, 'text_length': len(text_content), 'potential_nature_counts': list(found_numbers), 'pattern_matches': pattern_matches, 'tables_found': len(tables), 'relevant_tables': table_data, 'stat_keywords_found': found_keywords } analysis_results.append(file_analysis) except Exception as e: print(f"Error analyzing {filename}: {e}") analysis_results.append({ 'filename': filename, 'error': str(e) }) # Save comprehensive analysis analysis_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'nature_2020_content_analysis.json') with open(analysis_file, 'w') as f: json.dump({ 'analysis_timestamp': '2024-analysis', 'files_analyzed': len(html_files), 'analysis_results': analysis_results }, f, indent=2) print(f"\n=== ANALYSIS SUMMARY ===\n") print(f"Files analyzed: {len(html_files)}") print(f"Analysis results saved to: {analysis_file}") # Summary of findings all_potential_counts = set() all_keywords = set() total_tables = 0 for result in analysis_results: if 'potential_nature_counts' in result: all_potential_counts.update(result['potential_nature_counts']) if 'stat_keywords_found' in result: all_keywords.update(result['stat_keywords_found']) if 'tables_found' in result: total_tables += result['tables_found'] print(f"\n=== OVERALL FINDINGS ===\n") print(f"Total potential Nature article counts found: {sorted(all_potential_counts) if all_potential_counts else 'None'}") print(f"Total statistical keywords found: {len(all_keywords)}") print(f"Total tables analyzed: {total_tables}") if all_potential_counts: print(f"\n*** POTENTIAL NATURE 2020 ARTICLE COUNTS ***") for count in sorted(all_potential_counts): print(f" - {count} articles") else: print(f"\nNo specific Nature 2020 article counts were found in the downloaded sources.") print(f"Next approach: Try direct searches on Nature.com or Web of Science.") print(f"\n=== CONTENT ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===\n") print("Files created:") for file in os.listdir(workspace_dir): file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) if os.path.isfile(file_path): file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f" - {file} ({file_size:,} bytes)")

import os import requests import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import time import re print("=== DIRECT SEARCH FOR NATURE.COM 2020 PUBLICATION STATISTICS ===\n") # Create workspace directory os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Get API key api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found. Proceeding with direct Nature.com searches...\n") # More targeted search queries focusing on Nature.com official sources direct_nature_queries = [ 'site:nature.com "annual report" 2020 "research articles" OR "publications"', 'site:nature.com "about Nature" statistics 2020 articles published', 'site:nature.com "Nature journal" 2020 "number of articles" OR "article count"', 'site:nature.com "editorial" OR "metrics" 2020 publication statistics', '"Nature journal" "2020" "published" filetype:pdf annual report statistics' ] # Also try searches for Nature publishing group reports springer_nature_queries = [ 'site:springernature.com "Nature journal" 2020 "articles published" statistics', '"Springer Nature" annual report 2020 "Nature journal" publication count', 'site:springernature.com "publishing metrics" Nature 2020 research articles' ] # Combine all targeted queries all_targeted_queries = direct_nature_queries + springer_nature_queries print(f"Executing {len(all_targeted_queries)} targeted searches...\n") targeted_results = [] for i, query in enumerate(all_targeted_queries, 1): print(f"Search {i}/{len(all_targeted_queries)}: {query[:60]}...") params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 8, "type": "search" } try: response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f" Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results") # Analyze results for high-value targets high_value_results = [] for result in results['organic_results']: title = result.get('title', '').lower() snippet = result.get('snippet', '').lower() url = result.get('link', '').lower() # Score based on likelihood of containing Nature 2020 statistics value_score = 0 # High value indicators if 'annual report' in (title + snippet): value_score += 15 if 'nature.com' in url: value_score += 10 if 'springernature.com' in url: value_score += 10 if 'statistics' in (title + snippet): value_score += 8 if 'metrics' in (title + snippet): value_score += 7 if 'published' in (title + snippet) and '2020' in (title + snippet): value_score += 12 if 'articles' in (title + snippet) and 'count' in (title + snippet): value_score += 10 if '.pdf' in url: value_score += 5 if value_score >= 10: high_value_results.append({ 'title': result.get('title'), 'url': result.get('link'), 'snippet': result.get('snippet'), 'value_score': value_score, 'search_query': query }) targeted_results.extend(high_value_results) if high_value_results: print(f" *** {len(high_value_results)} high-value results identified ***") for result in high_value_results[:2]: print(f" Score {result['value_score']}: {result['title'][:60]}...") else: print(" No results found") else: print(f" Search failed with status {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f" Error in search {i}: {e}") time.sleep(1) print() # Sort all results by value score targeted_results.sort(key=lambda x: x['value_score'], reverse=True) print(f"=== HIGH-VALUE TARGETS IDENTIFIED ===\n") print(f"Found {len(targeted_results)} high-value targets (score >= 10)\n") # Display top targets for i, result in enumerate(targeted_results[:8], 1): print(f"Target {i} (Score: {result['value_score']})") print(f" Title: {result['title']}") print(f" URL: {result['url']}") print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet'][:120]}...") print(f" From query: {result['search_query'][:50]}...") print() # Save targeted search results targeted_search_file = 'workspace/nature_targeted_search_results.json' with open(targeted_search_file, 'w') as f: json.dump({ 'search_timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'total_queries': len(all_targeted_queries), 'high_value_targets': len(targeted_results), 'targeted_results': targeted_results }, f, indent=2) print(f"Targeted search results saved to: {targeted_search_file}") # Access the most promising targets if targeted_results: print(f"\n=== ACCESSING TOP TARGETS FOR NATURE 2020 DATA ===\n") headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Connection': 'keep-alive' } successful_accesses = [] # Try to access top 4 targets for i, target in enumerate(targeted_results[:4], 1): print(f"Accessing target {i}: {target['title'][:50]}...") print(f"URL: {target['url']}") try: response = requests.get(target['url'], headers=headers, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: print(f" ‚úì Successfully accessed (Status: {response.status_code})") print(f" Content length: {len(response.content):,} bytes") # Save content filename = f"workspace/nature_target_{i}_score_{target['value_score']}.html" with open(filename, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f" Content saved to: {filename}") # Quick analysis for 2020 publication data soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') text_content = soup.get_text().lower() # Look for Nature 2020 article statistics nature_2020_patterns = [ r'nature.*?journal.*?2020.*?(\d{3,4}).*?(?:articles?|research|publications?)', r'2020.*?nature.*?(\d{3,4}).*?(?:articles?|research|publications?)', r'(?:published|total).*?(\d{3,4}).*?(?:articles?|papers?).*?nature.*?2020', r'nature.*?2020.*?(?:published|total).*?(\d{3,4})', r'research.*?articles?.*?nature.*?2020.*?(\d{3,4})' ] potential_counts = set() contexts = [] for pattern in nature_2020_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, text_content) for match in matches: if 100 <= int(match) <= 9999: # Reasonable range for journal articles potential_counts.add(match) # Get context match_pos = text_content.find(match) if match_pos != -1: start = max(0, match_pos - 150) end = min(len(response.text), match_pos + 150) context = response.text[start:end].replace('\n', ' ').strip() contexts.append({ 'count': match, 'context': context }) if potential_counts: print(f" *** POTENTIAL NATURE 2020 COUNTS FOUND: {sorted(potential_counts)} ***") for ctx in contexts[:3]: print(f" Count {ctx['count']}: ...{ctx['context'][:100]}...") else: print(f" No specific Nature 2020 article counts detected") successful_accesses.append({ 'target_info': target, 'filename': filename, 'content_length': len(response.content), 'potential_counts': list(potential_counts), 'contexts': contexts }) else: print(f" ‚úó Access failed (Status: {response.status_code})") except Exception as e: print(f" ‚úó Error accessing: {e}") print() time.sleep(2) # Save access results access_summary = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'targets_attempted': min(4, len(targeted_results)), 'successful_accesses': len(successful_accesses), 'access_results': successful_accesses } access_file = 'workspace/nature_targeted_access_summary.json' with open(access_file, 'w') as f: json.dump(access_summary, f, indent=2) print(f"=== TARGETED ACCESS SUMMARY ===\n") print(f"Targets attempted: {access_summary['targets_attempted']}") print(f"Successful accesses: {len(successful_accesses)}") print(f"Access summary saved to: {access_file}") # Compile all potential counts found all_found_counts = set() for access in successful_accesses: all_found_counts.update(access['potential_counts']) if all_found_counts: print(f"\n*** COMPILATION OF POTENTIAL NATURE 2020 ARTICLE COUNTS ***") for count in sorted(all_found_counts, key=int): print(f" - {count} articles") print(f"\nMost likely candidates (based on typical journal ranges):") reasonable_counts = [c for c in all_found_counts if 200 <= int(c) <= 2000] if reasonable_counts: for count in sorted(reasonable_counts, key=int): print(f" ‚úì {count} articles (reasonable range)") else: print(f" No counts in typical journal range (200-2000) found") else: print(f"\nNo specific Nature 2020 article counts found in accessed targets.") else: print(f"No high-value targets identified for access.") print(f"\n=== DIRECT NATURE SEARCH COMPLETE ===\n") print("Files created in workspace/:") for file in os.listdir('workspace'): file_path = os.path.join('workspace', file) if os.path.isfile(file_path): file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f" - {file} ({file_size:,} bytes)") print(f"\nNext step: Analyze the targeted content for definitive Nature 2020 publication statistics")

import os import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re from collections import defaultdict print("=== COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS OF ALL EXISTING WORKSPACE CONTENT ===\n") # Find workspace directory workspace_dirs = [d for d in os.listdir('.') if d.startswith('workspace')] if not workspace_dirs: print("No workspace directory found.") exit() workspace_dir = workspace_dirs[0] print(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\n") # Get all files in workspace and categorize them all_files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) html_files = [f for f in all_files if f.endswith('.html')] json_files = [f for f in all_files if f.endswith('.json')] txt_files = [f for f in all_files if f.endswith('.txt')] print(f"Files in workspace:") print(f" HTML files: {len(html_files)} ({', '.join(html_files)})") print(f" JSON files: {len(json_files)} ({', '.join(json_files)})") print(f" TXT files: {len(txt_files)} ({', '.join(txt_files)})") # First, let's inspect any existing analysis files to understand what's been done print("\n=== INSPECTING EXISTING ANALYSIS FILES ===\n") for json_file in json_files: if 'analysis' in json_file.lower() or 'summary' in json_file.lower(): file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, json_file) file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f"Examining {json_file} ({file_size:,} bytes)") try: with open(file_path, 'r') as f: data = json.load(f) print(f" Structure: {type(data).__name__}") if isinstance(data, dict): print(f" Top-level keys: {list(data.keys())}") # Look for any mention of article counts or Nature statistics json_str = json.dumps(data).lower() if 'nature' in json_str and any(num in json_str for num in ['2020', 'articles', 'published']): print(f" *** Contains Nature-related data ***") print() except Exception as e: print(f" Error reading {json_file}: {e}\n") # Now systematically analyze ALL HTML files that haven't been thoroughly examined print("=== SYSTEMATIC ANALYSIS OF ALL HTML CONTENT ===\n") analysis_results = [] all_potential_counts = set() all_contexts = [] for html_file in html_files: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, html_file) file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f"Analyzing {html_file} ({file_size:,} bytes)") try: with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: html_content = f.read() # Parse with BeautifulSoup soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Extract basic info title_tag = soup.find('title') page_title = title_tag.get_text().strip() if title_tag else 'No title found' # Get all text content text_content = soup.get_text() text_lower = text_content.lower() print(f" Title: {page_title[:80]}...") print(f" Text length: {len(text_content):,} characters") # Enhanced search patterns specifically for Nature journal 2020 statistics enhanced_patterns = [ # Direct Nature journal patterns r'nature\s+(?:journal)?\s*(?:published|had|contained)\s*(?:a\s+total\s+of\s+)?(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?\s+(?:in\s+)?2020', r'(?:in\s+)?2020\s*,?\s*nature\s+(?:journal\s+)?(?:published|had|contained)\s+(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?', r'nature\s+(?:journal\s+)?2020\s*[:\-]?\s*(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?', r'(?:total\s+of\s+)?(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?\s+(?:were\s+)?published\s+(?:in\s+)?nature\s+(?:journal\s+)?(?:in\s+)?2020', # Annual report patterns r'(?:annual\s+report|statistics).*?nature.*?2020.*?(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?', r'nature.*?(?:annual\s+report|statistics).*?2020.*?(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?', # Publication metrics patterns r'nature\s+(?:journal\s+)?(?:metrics|statistics|impact).*?2020.*?(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?', r'(?:journal\s+)?metrics.*?nature.*?2020.*?(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?', # Volume/issue patterns r'nature\s+(?:volume|vol)\s+\d+.*?2020.*?(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?', r'2020\s+volume\s+\d+.*?nature.*?(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?', # Citation database patterns r'(?:web\s+of\s+science|scopus|pubmed).*?nature.*?2020.*?(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?', r'nature.*?(?:web\s+of\s+science|scopus|pubmed).*?2020.*?(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?' ] file_potential_counts = set() file_contexts = [] # Apply each pattern for pattern in enhanced_patterns: matches = re.finditer(pattern, text_lower, re.IGNORECASE | re.DOTALL) for match in matches: count = match.group(1) # Filter for reasonable article counts (Nature typically publishes 800-1200 research articles per year) if 200 <= int(count) <= 3000: file_potential_counts.add(count) all_potential_counts.add(count) # Get extended context match_start = max(0, match.start() - 200) match_end = min(len(text_content), match.end() + 200) context = text_content[match_start:match_end].replace('\n', ' ').strip() context_info = { 'file': html_file, 'count': count, 'pattern': pattern, 'context': context, 'confidence': 'high' if 'nature' in context.lower() and '2020' in context else 'medium' } file_contexts.append(context_info) all_contexts.append(context_info) # Also search for any tables that might contain Nature statistics tables = soup.find_all('table') table_findings = [] for i, table in enumerate(tables): table_text = table.get_text().lower() if 'nature' in table_text and ('2020' in table_text or 'articles' in table_text): # Extract table data rows = table.find_all('tr') table_data = [] for row in rows[:5]: # First 5 rows cells = [cell.get_text().strip() for cell in row.find_all(['td', 'th'])] if cells: table_data.append(cells) table_findings.append({ 'table_index': i, 'table_data': table_data }) # Look for specific Nature journal mentions with numbers nature_mentions = [] nature_pattern = r'nature\s+(?:journal)?[^.]{0,100}?(\d{2,4})[^.]{0,100}?(?:articles?|papers?|publications?)' nature_matches = re.finditer(nature_pattern, text_lower, re.IGNORECASE) for match in nature_matches: number = match.group(1) if 100 <= int(number) <= 5000: context_start = max(0, match.start() - 100) context_end = min(len(text_content), match.end() + 100) mention_context = text_content[context_start:context_end].replace('\n', ' ').strip() nature_mentions.append({ 'number': number, 'context': mention_context }) print(f" Potential counts found: {sorted(file_potential_counts) if file_potential_counts else 'None'}") print(f" Nature mentions with numbers: {len(nature_mentions)}") print(f" Relevant tables: {len(table_findings)}") if file_potential_counts: print(f" *** HIGH PRIORITY: Contains potential Nature 2020 counts ***") for ctx in file_contexts[:2]: # Show top 2 contexts print(f" Count {ctx['count']} ({ctx['confidence']}): ...{ctx['context'][:120]}...") # Store analysis results analysis_results.append({ 'filename': html_file, 'file_size': file_size, 'page_title': page_title, 'text_length': len(text_content), 'potential_counts': list(file_potential_counts), 'contexts': file_contexts, 'nature_mentions': nature_mentions, 'relevant_tables': table_findings }) except Exception as e: print(f" Error analyzing {html_file}: {e}") analysis_results.append({ 'filename': html_file, 'error': str(e) }) print() # Comprehensive summary print("=== COMPREHENSIVE FINDINGS SUMMARY ===\n") # Count frequency analysis count_frequency = defaultdict(int) for ctx in all_contexts: count_frequency[ctx['count']] += 1 print(f"Total HTML files analyzed: {len(html_files)}") print(f"Total potential Nature 2020 counts found: {len(all_potential_counts)}") print(f"Total contexts with potential counts: {len(all_contexts)}") if all_potential_counts: print(f"\n*** ALL POTENTIAL NATURE 2020 ARTICLE COUNTS ***") for count in sorted(all_potential_counts, key=int): frequency = count_frequency[count] print(f" {count} articles (found {frequency} time{'s' if frequency > 1 else ''})") # Highlight most frequent/credible counts print(f"\n*** MOST CREDIBLE CANDIDATES (based on frequency and context) ***") credible_counts = [(count, freq) for count, freq in count_frequency.items() if freq > 1 or 800 <= int(count) <= 1500] if credible_counts: for count, freq in sorted(credible_counts, key=lambda x: (x[1], int(x[0])), reverse=True): print(f" ‚úì {count} articles (frequency: {freq}, in typical Nature range)") # Show best contexts for this count relevant_contexts = [ctx for ctx in all_contexts if ctx['count'] == count and ctx['confidence'] == 'high'] if relevant_contexts: best_context = relevant_contexts[0] print(f" Context: ...{best_context['context'][:150]}...") print(f" Source: {best_context['file']}") else: print(f" No highly credible counts identified based on frequency/range criteria") else: print(f"\nNo specific Nature 2020 article counts found in any of the downloaded content.") # Save comprehensive analysis final_analysis = { 'analysis_timestamp': '2024-comprehensive-analysis', 'files_analyzed': len(html_files), 'total_potential_counts': len(all_potential_counts), 'count_frequency': dict(count_frequency), 'all_potential_counts': sorted(all_potential_counts, key=int), 'detailed_results': analysis_results, 'high_confidence_contexts': [ctx for ctx in all_contexts if ctx['confidence'] == 'high'], 'credible_candidates': credible_counts if 'credible_counts' in locals() else [] } final_analysis_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'comprehensive_nature_2020_analysis.json') with open(final_analysis_file, 'w') as f: json.dump(final_analysis, f, indent=2) print(f"\n=== ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===\n") print(f"Comprehensive analysis saved to: {final_analysis_file}") if all_potential_counts: print(f"\n*** FINAL RECOMMENDATION ***") if credible_counts: top_candidate = max(credible_counts, key=lambda x: (x[1], int(x[0]) if 800 <= int(x[0]) <= 1500 else 0)) print(f"Most likely Nature 2020 research article count: {top_candidate[0]} articles") print(f"Confidence level: {'High' if top_candidate[1] > 1 else 'Medium'} (found {top_candidate[1]} time(s))") else: reasonable_counts = [c for c in all_potential_counts if 800 <= int(c) <= 1500] if reasonable_counts: print(f"Reasonable candidates in typical Nature range: {sorted(reasonable_counts, key=int)}") else: print(f"No counts found in typical Nature journal range (800-1500 articles/year)") else: print(f"\n*** CONCLUSION ***") print(f"No definitive Nature journal 2020 research article counts found in available content.") print(f"Alternative approaches needed: direct Nature.com access or bibliometric databases.")

Show best contexts for this count relevant_contexts = [ctx for ctx in all_contexts if ctx['count'] == count and ctx['confidence'] == 'high'] if relevant_contexts: best_context = relevant_contexts[0] print(f" Context: ...{best_context['context'][:150]}...") print(f" Source: {best_context['file']}") else: print(f" No highly credible counts identified based on frequency/range criteria") else: print(f"\nNo specific Nature 2020 article counts found in any of the downloaded content.") # Save comprehensive analysis final_analysis = { 'analysis_timestamp': '2024-comprehensive-analysis', 'files_analyzed': len(html_files), 'total_potential_counts': len(all_potential_counts), 'count_frequency': dict(count_frequency), 'all_potential_counts': sorted(all_potential_counts, key=int), 'detailed_results': analysis_results, 'high_confidence_contexts': [ctx for ctx in all_contexts if ctx['confidence'] == 'high'], 'credible_candidates': credible_counts if 'credible_counts' in locals() else [] } final_analysis_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'comprehensive_nature_2020_analysis.json') with open(final_analysis_file, 'w') as f: json.dump(final_analysis, f, indent=2) print(f"\n=== ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===\n") print(f"Comprehensive analysis saved to: {final_analysis_file}") if all_potential_counts: print(f"\n*** FINAL RECOMMENDATION ***") if credible_counts: top_candidate = max(credible_counts, key=lambda x: (x[1], int(x[0]) if 800 <= int(x[0]) <= 1500 else 0)) print(f"Most likely Nature 2020 research article count: {top_candidate[0]} articles") print(f"Confidence level: {'High' if top_candidate[1] > 1 else 'Medium'} (found {top_candidate[1]} time(s))") else: reasonable_counts = [c for c in all_potential_counts if 800 <= int(c) <= 1500] if reasonable_counts: print(f"Reasonable candidates in typical Nature range: {sorted(reasonable_counts, key=int)}") else: print(f"No counts found in typical Nature journal range (800-1500 articles/year)") else: print(f"\n*** CONCLUSION ***") print(f"No definitive Nature journal 2020 research article counts found in available content.") print(f"Alternative approaches needed: direct Nature.com access or bibliometric databases.")

import os import requests import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re import time print("=== ALTERNATIVE APPROACH: ACCESSING NATURE'S OFFICIAL STATISTICS PAGES ===\n") # Create workspace directory os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # The previous analysis incorrectly identified '2021' as an article count when it's actually a year # Let's try a different approach: access Nature.com directly for official statistics print("Previous analysis error detected: '2021' is a year, not an article count.") print("Switching to direct Nature.com access for official publication statistics...\n") # Try to access Nature's official pages that might contain 2020 statistics official_nature_urls = [ 'https://www.nature.com/nature/volumes', # Nature volumes page 'https://www.nature.com/nature/articles?type=article&year=2020', # Direct 2020 articles 'https://www.nature.com/nature/about', # About Nature page 'https://www.nature.com/nature/journal-information', # Journal information 'https://www.springernature.com/gp/group/annual-report' # Springer Nature annual report ] headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Connection': 'keep-alive' } successful_accesses = [] for i, url in enumerate(official_nature_urls, 1): print(f"Accessing official Nature URL {i}/{len(official_nature_urls)}:") print(f"URL: {url}") try: response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: print(f" ‚úì Successfully accessed (Status: {response.status_code})") print(f" Content length: {len(response.content):,} bytes") # Save the content filename = f"workspace/nature_official_{i}.html" with open(filename, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f" Content saved to: {filename}") # Quick analysis for 2020 publication data soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') text_content = soup.get_text().lower() # Look for specific patterns that indicate article counts count_patterns = [ r'(?:published|total)\s+(?:of\s+)?(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?\s+(?:in\s+)?2020', r'2020\s*[:\-]?\s*(?:published|total)?\s*(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?', r'volume\s+\d+\s*\(2020\)\s*[:\-]?\s*(\d{3,4})\s+(?:research\s+)?articles?', r'(?:articles?\s+count|publication\s+statistics)\s*[:\-]?\s*(\d{3,4})\s*(?:for\s+)?2020' ] potential_counts = set() contexts = [] for pattern in count_patterns: matches = re.finditer(pattern, text_content) for match in matches: count = match.group(1) if 500 <= int(count) <= 2000: # Reasonable range for Nature potential_counts.add(count) # Get context start = max(0, match.start() - 150) end = min(len(response.text), match.end() + 150) context = response.text[start:end].replace('\n', ' ').strip() contexts.append({ 'count': count, 'context': context }) # Also look for any mention of Nature's 2020 volume information volume_pattern = r'nature\s+volume\s+(\d+)\s*\(2020\)' volume_matches = re.findall(volume_pattern, text_content, re.IGNORECASE) # Look for issue numbers which might help estimate article count issue_pattern = r'(?:issues?|numbers?)\s*[:\-]?\s*(\d+)\s*[-‚Äì]\s*(\d+)' issue_matches = re.findall(issue_pattern, text_content) print(f" Potential article counts: {sorted(potential_counts) if potential_counts else 'None'}") print(f" Volume information: {volume_matches if volume_matches else 'None'}") print(f" Issue ranges: {issue_matches if issue_matches else 'None'}") if potential_counts: print(f" *** POTENTIAL COUNTS FOUND ***") for ctx in contexts[:2]: print(f" Count {ctx['count']}: ...{ctx['context'][:100]}...") successful_accesses.append({ 'url': url, 'filename': filename, 'content_length': len(response.content), 'potential_counts': list(potential_counts), 'contexts': contexts, 'volume_info': volume_matches, 'issue_info': issue_matches }) else: print(f" ‚úó Access failed (Status: {response.status_code})") except Exception as e: print(f" ‚úó Error accessing: {e}") print() time.sleep(2) # Respectful delay # Try an alternative approach: look for Nature's 2020 volume page directly print("=== TRYING DIRECT VOLUME ACCESS ===\n") # Nature typically publishes weekly, so volume 588 was 2020 volume_urls = [ 'https://www.nature.com/nature/volumes/588', # Nature volume 588 (2020) 'https://www.nature.com/nature/volumes/587', # Nature volume 587 (2020) 'https://www.nature.com/nature/volumes/589' # Nature volume 589 (2021, for comparison) ] volume_data = [] for i, volume_url in enumerate(volume_urls, 1): print(f"Accessing Nature volume {i}/{len(volume_urls)}:") print(f"URL: {volume_url}") try: response = requests.get(volume_url, headers=headers, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: print(f" ‚úì Successfully accessed volume page") soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for article listings or counts article_links = soup.find_all('a', href=re.compile(r'/articles/')) research_articles = [link for link in article_links if 'research' in link.get_text().lower() or 'article' in link.get('href', '')] # Look for issue information issue_info = soup.find_all(text=re.compile(r'issue|number', re.IGNORECASE)) print(f" Article links found: {len(article_links)}") print(f" Potential research articles: {len(research_articles)}") if len(research_articles) > 0: print(f" Sample research articles:") for article in research_articles[:3]: print(f" - {article.get_text()[:60]}...") volume_data.append({ 'url': volume_url, 'total_links': len(article_links), 'research_articles': len(research_articles), 'volume_number': volume_url.split('/')[-1] }) else: print(f" ‚úó Failed to access volume (Status: {response.status_code})") except Exception as e: print(f" ‚úó Error accessing volume: {e}") print() time.sleep(2) # Save results results_summary = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'approach': 'Direct Nature.com official page access', 'official_pages_accessed': len(successful_accesses), 'volume_pages_checked': len(volume_data), 'official_access_results': successful_accesses, 'volume_analysis': volume_data } results_file = 'workspace/nature_official_access_results.json' with open(results_file, 'w') as f: json.dump(results_summary, f, indent=2) print(f"=== OFFICIAL ACCESS SUMMARY ===\n") print(f"Official Nature pages accessed: {len(successful_accesses)}") print(f"Volume pages analyzed: {len(volume_data)}") print(f"Results saved to: {results_file}") # Compile findings all_potential_counts = set() for access in successful_accesses: all_potential_counts.update(access['potential_counts']) if all_potential_counts: print(f"\n*** POTENTIAL NATURE 2020 ARTICLE COUNTS FROM OFFICIAL SOURCES ***") for count in sorted(all_potential_counts, key=int): print(f" - {count} articles") # Show contexts for verification print(f"\n*** VERIFICATION CONTEXTS ***") for access in successful_accesses: if access['contexts']: print(f"From {access['url']}:") for ctx in access['contexts'][:1]: print(f" Count {ctx['count']}: ...{ctx['context'][:120]}...") else: print(f"\nNo specific article counts found in official Nature pages.") # Alternative: estimate from volume data if available if volume_data: print(f"\n*** VOLUME-BASED ESTIMATION ***") for vol in volume_data: if vol['research_articles'] > 0: print(f"Volume {vol['volume_number']}: ~{vol['research_articles']} research articles found") # If we have data from volume 588 (2020), estimate annual count vol_588_data = next((v for v in volume_data if v['volume_number'] == '588'), None) if vol_588_data and vol_588_data['research_articles'] > 0: # Nature publishes ~52 issues per year, estimate based on sample estimated_annual = vol_588_data['research_articles'] * 52 // 10 # Rough estimation print(f"\nEstimated 2020 research articles (very rough): ~{estimated_annual}") print(f"\n=== DIRECT NATURE ACCESS COMPLETE ===\n") print("Alternative approaches if needed:") print("1. Contact Nature directly for official statistics") print("2. Access Web of Science or Scopus databases with institutional access") print("3. Search for Nature's annual report or editorial statements about 2020 publishing")
